.PHP Class ^2wyq5ojJ

.PHP Class ^b9fFBYt1

If -> Saving Data:
1. Sanitize read string.
2. Validate: Correct data type.
3. Connect to Data Layer.
4. Rise and save data in DB.

If -> Reading Data:
1. Connect to Data Layer.
2. Convert data to Strings.
3. If data has no context: 
-> Look for context in other tables.
4. Run Analytics.
5. Return resulting data. ^q6QcOG9B

.PHP Class ^JzFyzbix

and a PHP Page Template and returns it to our
home.php. ^BX6ajXfC

create all the necessary data for charts. ^cfij9PD5

RECOLECTION gets all country names, IDs and
nationalities from RestCountries.API ^e13ET6vT

.PHP Class ^1dO5D3vG

Si voy a guardar datos:
  1. Sanitizar la cadena
  2. Validar que los datos sean 
      correctos.
  3. Conectarme a la Base de Datos y
      Enviar lo recolectado.

Si voy a mostrar datos: 
   1. Convertir la data de la base a
      Datos legibles por las personas
   2. Sanitizar y Retornar datos ^1JmxcvE1
